Online Supporting Information S1. The benchmark dataset S = SAMP Snon-AMP ,
where SAMP contains 1,388 AMP sequences while Snon-AMP contains 1,440 non-AMP
sequences. The AMP sequences are further classified into four subsets according to
their attributes, i.e., SAMP = S1
AMP S2
AMP S3
AMP S4
AMP , where S1
AMP contains 1,274
antibacterial peptides, S2
AMP 101 anticancer/tumor peptides, S3
AMP 481 antifungal
peptides, and S4
AMP 102 antiviral peptides. A sequence in SAMP may belong to more
than one attribute. Of the 1,388 AMP sequences, 912 belong to one attribute, 385 to
two attributes, 80 to three attributes, and 11 to four attributes.
I. SAMP : 1,388 AMP sequences
(1) S1
AMP : 1,274 antibacterial peptides
